# Romanian translation status 


## Flarum core

| Component | Status |
| --- | --- |
| [Core](https://github.com/flarum/core) | [![Translation status](https://weblate.rob006.net/widgets/flarum/ro/core/svg-badge.svg)](https://weblate.rob006.net/projects/flarum/core/ro/) |
| Validation | [![Translation status](https://weblate.rob006.net/widgets/flarum/ro/validation/svg-badge.svg)](https://weblate.rob006.net/projects/flarum/validation/ro/) |
